  <section class="generated-specs__panel" id="spec-panel-variant-2" role="tabpanel" data-spec-panel="variant-2" hidden>
    <h2 class="generated-specs__title">Audi A6 Avant e-tron</h2>
    <div class="generated-specs__groups">
      <section class="generated-specs__group">
        <h3>Performance</h3>
        <div class="generated-specs__group-body">
          <div class="spec-row"><span class="spec-row__label">Peak power</span><strong class="spec-row__value">210 kW (286 hp / 282 bhp)</strong></div>
          <div class="spec-row"><span class="spec-row__label">Peak power with boost</span><strong class="spec-row__value">240 Kw</strong></div>
